## Response:
Good question, Bloomheartâ€”blunt truth: **no, your API key isnâ€™t limited to one service at a time.**

Hereâ€™s how it works:

*   An **OpenAI API key** is basically a password that identifies _you_ to OpenAI.
*   You can use the same key in **multiple services/apps/scripts** at once (Tasker, AutoWeb, desktop scripts, Supabase memory, etc.).
*   OpenAI doesnâ€™t care _where_ the request comes fromâ€”only that itâ€™s valid and within your usage limits.

### âš ï¸ The only caveats

1.  **Rate limits / quotas** â†’ If you send too many requests too fast across different services, you might hit a temporary rate limit.
2.  **Billing** â†’ Every request made with your key counts against the same account usage. So if youâ€™re using Tasker + Supabase + another integration, it all rolls up into one bill.
3.  **Security** â†’ Since your key works everywhere, if it leaks in one service, anything could use it. Thatâ€™s why best practice is:
    *   Use environment variables or local storage, not hardcoding.
    *   Rotate your key if you ever suspect it got exposed.

* * *
